      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 12th century
       </b>
       . During the period 1101 to 1200 there were 250
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 92 were
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Types" title="Solar eclipse">
        partial
       </a>
       , 82 were annular, 61 were total, and 15 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 17 different years: 1103, 1110, 1114, 1117, 1121, 1125, 1132, 1139, 1150, 1157, 1168, 1175, 1179, 1182, 1186, 1190, and 1197. One month, March 1150, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
